    function pushAdTag(view_config, orientation, container_id) {
        if (typeof view_config[app_nexus.view] === 'number') {
            window._aeq = window._aeq || [];

            if (container_id == 'contentad-outstream-1') {
                window._aeq.push(['getAdTag', 'VIDEO_OUTSTREAM', 'contentad-outstream-1']);
            } else {
                window._aeq.push(['getAdTag', {
                    containerId: container_id,
                    orientation: orientation,
                    index: view_config[app_nexus.view],
                }]);
            }
        }
    }

    window.app_nexus = [];

    var viewportWidth = Math.max(document.documentElement.clientWidth, window.innerWidth || 0);

    if (viewportWidth < 660) {
        app_nexus.view = "smartphone";
    } else if (viewportWidth < 1000) {
        app_nexus.view = "tablet";
    } else {
        app_nexus.view = "desktop";
    }

    if (app_nexus.view != "desktop") {
        app_nexus.mobile = true;
    } else {
        app_nexus.mobile = false;
    }

    var globalOptions = {"layout":"homepage","category":"home","adunit1":"chip_digital","adunit2":"home","keyword":"chipbrandhub, brandhub, nooutbrain, nopolar"};

    globalOptions.mobile = app_nexus.mobile;

    window._aeq = window._aeq || [];
    window._aeq.push(['setGlobalOptions', globalOptions]);

<script>
    var rand = Math.round(Math.random() * 10e2),
        writeCookie,
        readCookie;

    writeCookie = function(name, value, expires, path) {
        value = encodeURIComponent(value);
        expires = expires || null; // in seconds

        var stringToSet = name + '=' + value;

        if (expires !== null) {
            var date = new Date();
            date = new Date(date.getTime() + 1000 * expires);

            stringToSet += ';expires=' + date.toUTCString();
        }

        if (typeof path === 'undefined') {
            path = '/';
        }

        if (path !== '') {
            stringToSet += ';path=' + path;
        }

        document.cookie = stringToSet;
    };

    readCookie = function(cookie) {
        var content = '',
            name = '',
            start,
            end;

        if (document.cookie.length > 0) {
            name = cookie + '=';
            start = document.cookie.indexOf(name);
            end = 0;

            if (start > -1) {
                start += name.length;
                end = document.cookie.indexOf(';', start);

                if (end < start) {
                    end = document.cookie.length;
                }

                content = document.cookie.substring(start, end);
            }
        }

        return decodeURIComponent(content);
    };

    if (readCookie('AB_SegmentNew') === '') {
        if (rand <= 49) {
            writeCookie('AB_SegmentNew', 'nosourcepoint', 2592000); // g detection
        } else {
            writeCookie('AB_SegmentNew', 'sourcepoint', 2592000); // sp detection
        }
    }

    if (readCookie('AB_countNew') === '') {
        writeCookie('AB_countNew', 'first', 2592000);
    } else {
        writeCookie('AB_countNew', 'notfirst', 2592000);
    }

    if ((readCookie('AB_SegmentNew') === 'sourcepoint' || document.location.href.indexOf('forceSourcepoint') !== -1)) {
